              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1800698776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15904585586973441821">This series is one of those type of books that make it impossible to explain what actually happened and how I felt about. Let me just tell you that I'm in love with this series and completely obsessed with it. I can't seem to put these books down and I'm always itching to find out what happens next. <br/><br/>I'm actually so sad that I have to wait for my copy of Crystal Storm to arrived. I'm so not ready to leave this world for longer than a few days. Also, how will I cope with a whole year before the ep</span>
  <span id="freeText15904585586973441821" style="display:none">This series is one of those type of books that make it impossible to explain what actually happened and how I felt about. Let me just tell you that I'm in love with this series and completely obsessed with it. I can't seem to put these books down and I'm always itching to find out what happens next. <br /><br />I'm actually so sad that I have to wait for my copy of Crystal Storm to arrived. I'm so not ready to leave this world for longer than a few days. Also, how will I cope with a whole year before the epic conclusion next December?! I hate myself for getting caught up so quickly!!! <br /><br />The last 40% of this book was incredible, however the first 60% was a bit slow paced. This cover is my absolute favourite, even though I grew to loathe this particular character. There will be some spoilers in this review but I'll try my best to mark the big ones - general ones such as ships will not be marked so BEWARE.<br /><br />There was a certain event that occurred in this book that left me feeling a bit meh. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Going into Frozen Tides, I was aware that someone was going to die. I'd seen it in status updates and a friend of mine hinted that it would happen. From what I had seen, it was someone that no one really cared for so I instantly assumed it was Jonas because I've seen a lot of negative reviews about him. However, it was in fact Lysandra who was burned to death and vanished? I'm kinda confused about her death and it was utterly <b><i>pointless</i></b>. Honestly, I only started liking her as a character because of her name (same as Lysandra from the Throne of Glass series) so I wasn't too concerned by her death.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Magnus and Cleo will forever remain my favourite characters in this book so I'm beyond ecstatic that they are a ship. <b>I will go down with the Magneo ship </b><s>and no one can stop me.</s><br />If you want a sum up of this ship:<br /><br /><i>"Sometimes I think you make it your daily task to confuse me."<br />"The feeling is entirely mutual, princess."</i><br /><br />LITERALLY THEY ARE SO CONFUSING AND SO BACK AND FORTH AND I NEED THEM TO SHUT UP AND JUST LOVE EACH OTHER UNCONDITIONALLY ALREADY.<br /><br /><i>"He didn't deserve her; he knew he didn't. He was the Prince of Blood, the son of a monster, who said and did cruel things. Who preemptively leapt to hurt anyone before they could hurt him first. But he would show her that he would change. Magnus could change for her."</i><br /><br />Honestly there's something about the 'enemies to lovers' love story that makes me ship it so hard it hurts. <i>I just need them to be happy okay</i><br /><br />Jonas is a hot mess and I don't even know where to begin to talk about him. I definitely grew to like him a lot more in this one. I've always liked him as a characters but he's been so irrational in the past 3 books and I think he's starting to find his chill.<br /><br />LUCIA WHAT THE FUCK HAS BEEN GOING ON WITH YOU GIRLFRIEND?! I really liked Lucia but damn she's a bitch for a lot of this book. I went from loving her to hating her and now I'm back to liking her again. She want through a lot in this book and damn I feel for her. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I CANT BELIEVE SHE'S PREGNANT!!!!!! I SCREAMED WHEN I SAW THAT. I'm so interested to see what happens from here - will she have the baby? what's going to happen now that she's in the sanctuary???? I need some answers asap!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />The King is a prick and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I can't believe he actually had a heart with some really fucked up motives. Also, Magnus isn't Sabina's child???? What???? Why is he lying all the time? I can't trust a word he says tbh.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I'M JUST SO HAPPY BECAUSE I CAN FINALLY READ THE BLURB OF BOOK 5 BECAUSE I WAS TOLD I WASN'T ALLOWED TO READ IT SINCE THERE WERE BIG SPOILERS IN IT. <br /><br />I say this every time, but READ THIS BOOK. Read this series. <s>
  <i>Don't talk to me unless you do.</i>
</s></span>

<div id="review_1796111113" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1796111113" />
    <a title="Cindy ✩☽♔" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3222333-cindy"><img alt="Cindy ✩☽♔" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605643833p2/3222333.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1796111113?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cindy ✩☽♔" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cindy ✩☽♔" href="/user/show/3222333-cindy">Cindy ✩☽♔</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=otps-feels">otps-feels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=kick-ass-heroines">kick-ass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1796111113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1126667860014610206"><b> “Because if you don't choose to fight against the wrong in the world, then you are the wrong in the world.”<br/>---<br/>“If every mortal looked at others as their friends, not as their enemies, the world would be a much better place, wouldn’t it?” </b><br/><br/>This series just keeps getting better and better! This is, without a doubt, my favorite book in the series. <br/><br/>A high-stakes, action-packed journey filled with secrets, betrayal, hate, love, forgiveness and redemption. <br/><br/>This story just keeps building and building, </span>
  <span id="freeText1126667860014610206" style="display:none"><b> “Because if you don't choose to fight against the wrong in the world, then you are the wrong in the world.”<br>---<br>“If every mortal looked at others as their friends, not as their enemies, the world would be a much better place, wouldn’t it?” </b><br><br>This series just keeps getting better and better! This is, without a doubt, my favorite book in the series. <br><br>A high-stakes, action-packed journey filled with secrets, betrayal, hate, love, forgiveness and redemption. <br><br>This story just keeps building and building, and just when you think it has finally reached it's climax another twist gets thrown into the mix. And the relationships? They are literally all over the place. Everyone, everything, is connected. There is no doubt that our characters will continue to be faced with endless challenges and forced to make difficult decisions. Which one leaves us to wonder, what will they chooses? And who will survive to see the end of this war? <br><br>On a happier note: <br>Magnus &amp; Cleo!!!<br><i> “I love you, Cleo,” he said, the words finally coming to him, with no effort at all because of how true they were. “I love you so much it hurts.”<br>Her eyes widened. “What did you just say?”<br>Magnus almost laughed. “I think you heard me right.” <br>---<br>He didn't deserve her; he knew didn't. He was the Prince of Blood, the son of a monster, who said and did cruel things. Who preemptively leapt to hurt anyone before they could hurt him first. <br>But he would show her that he could change. <br>Magnus could change for her. <br>She was his princess. No. She was his goddess. With her golden skin and golden hair. She was his light. His life. His everything.<br>He loved her more than anything else in this world. </i> <br><a href="http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/cincin1993/media/tumblr_o08wziUiRy1tvh39bo1_500_zpskaxtj2ph.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1477955842ra/21013233.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_o08wziUiRy1tvh39bo1_500_zpskaxtj2ph.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I ship these two so much! It is so strange because honestly their relationship has often been so terribly frustrating. Both of them spent so much time constantly denying their feelings for each other, clinging to their masks and pushing each other away. But at long last it seems progress has finally been made. In reality, I am not sure I'd be able to cheer on such a volatile relationship. These two are like fire and ice, a tornado and a volcano. It should not work, but it does. <br><br>Bonus content, Magnus being the Prince of Sass:<br><i> "You're not wearing a cloak. You'll freeze to death out here."<br>"Would you like that? Very sorry to disappoint you, but I'll be fine. Perhaps it's my cold, black heart that makes all the difference?"<br>---<br>"For now. But you should remember that charm opens far more doors than harsh words do."<br>"And a sharp ax will open every door." </i><br><br>Relationship Roadmap (events are not listed in any particular order) <br>Alrighty, here we go! <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br>Felix had/has feelings for Lysandra but has since hooked up with Amara, who also hooked up with Magnus <br><br>Amara killed her brother Ashur, who seemed to have a thing for Nic<br><br>Nic had/has longed loved Cleo. However, he may have also have feelings for Ashur who everyone believes is dead. By Cleo's request Nic went on a quest with Lysandra, Olivia and Jonas <br><br>Lysandra loves/loved Jonas, who does seemed to have some feelings for her but he also had/has feelings Cleo. But that all changed when Lysandra sacrificed herself to save Jonas, and now it seems he only sees Cleo as a friend.<br><br>Cleo also somewhat liked/likes Jonas, but she is also in love with Magnus. <br><br>Magnus it seems to have finally gotten over is love/lust for is adopted sister, and is now devoted to Cleo<br><br>Lucia never loved Magnus romantically. But is fiercely protective of him, though she often treated him like shit. Lucia loved Alexius, who is now dead after having killed himself to save Lucia. Thus, defying his orders from Melenia.<br><br>Melenia is a wicked Watcher who basically wanted to kill everyone in an attempt to release/rescue her lover Kyan. But, Kyan never loved her and instead wanted her dead. And then joined forces with Lucia to destroy Timotheus and possibly the world. <br><br>Timotheus is now the only remainer Elder Watcher, who sent Olivia to protect Jonas and visits Lucia in her dreams in attempts to sway her toward the right path? <br><br>Lucia despite all odds deeply misses not only her brother, but also her ruthless father King Gaus. Who somehow was always kind to her. <br><br>King Gaus seems to be on an endless quest to control and conquer - more like destroy - everything. But turns out he wasn't always that way, because once upon a time he was also a boy who would've done anything for love. And who was this mystery lady love you ask? Well it appears it was Cleo's mother. Yup, that's right. Maybe the apple does not fall far from the tree after all. This revelation all began with a brief conversation between King Gaius and his new wife, Amara. <br><br>Amara was forced to marry the King, but used the celebration to essentially kill her entire family. Then she framed their murders on Felix, who she was starting to fall in love with. Nice. Real nice of you Amara. <br><br>Felix was on the verge of being tortured to death until he was rescued by Jonas, a friend/comrade with whom he had a falling out due to his history of working for King Gaus. But thankfully all is forgiven, and they are friends again. He is then healed by Olivia and ready to head back to Mytica with Jonas and Nic. <br><br>However, just before they leave, Nic is introduced to Taran who happens to be Theon's twin brother. Not only that but he sees another familiar face, the supposedly dead prince! <br><br>Theon was Cleo's first love, who happened to have been killed by Magnus wayyyy back in book one. And now his brother vows revenge on Magnus.<br><a href="http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/cincin1993/media/raw_zpsicgyw0po.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1477950828ra/21012911.gif" alt=" photo raw_zpsicgyw0po.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>How will Cleo react when she comes face to face with the man who shares her dead lover's face? Will Cleo and Magnus survive all the obstacles that stand to tear them apart? <br><br>Will Nic finally get over his feelings for Cleo, once and for all? <br><br>Will Jonas finally come up with a successful plan? (From the looks of the synopsis for the 5th book, I think not. Especially if he is actually joining up with Lucia) <br><br>Will Lucia finally do something to make like her? (Turning her back on Kyan was definitely a start)<br><br>Will Felix succeed in getting his revenge on Amara and hopefully find happiness? (I hope so. Maybe Olivia?) <br><br>Is King Gaius actually going to be a changed man in the next book? <br><br>So many questions ahead, can't wait to see how it all goes down. <br>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>I think what makes this book the strongest among the bunch is that it finally connecting the dots between all the characters and plot points. People have finally showed their true selves, and now it's just matter of what all their decisions up until this point will mean for their futures and the futures of those around them. I also like the pacing in this book a lot better. There is always something of consequence happening, moving the narrative along at a steady pace. <br><br>All-in-all a highly entertaining read.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1466480405" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1466480405" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1466480405?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=witches">witches</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1466480405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5606511761162731689">1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1455382903' rel='nofollow noopener'>Falling Kingdoms</a> ★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470781684?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rebel Spring</a> ★★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1471808405?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Gathering Darkness</a> ★★★★★<br/><br/><i>“Because if you don't choose to fight against the wrong in the world, then you are the wrong in the world. ” </i><br/><br/>These books, somehow, just keep getting better and better. <b>This book was phenomenal.</b> This series is, hands down, the best series I've read in 2015. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1473732651?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>The fifth book</a> very quickly became one of my most anticipated reads of 2016.<br/><br/>Each book in this series always starts with a map. Every book the map gets bigger and bigger, a</span>
  <span id="freeText5606511761162731689" style="display:none">1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1455382903" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470781684?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Rebel Spring</a> ★★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1471808405?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Gathering Darkness</a> ★★★★★<br><br><i>“Because if you don't choose to fight against the wrong in the world, then you are the wrong in the world. ” </i><br><br>These books, somehow, just keep getting better and better. <b>This book was phenomenal.</b> This series is, hands down, the best series I've read in 2015. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1473732651?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The fifth book</a> very quickly became one of my most anticipated reads of 2016.<br><br>Each book in this series always starts with a map. Every book the map gets bigger and bigger, allowing you to see more of the surrounding areas of Mytica. The map in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1471808405?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Gathering Darkness</a> teaches us about Kraeshia, and how Mytica won't be on the only land mass in this six book story, but the map in <i>Frozen Tides</i> really makes the reader realize how small Mytica really is. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450578060i/17445542.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In this book, we are still following the main four characters. <b>Cleo</b> is still the star, in my opinion, and really shows how amazing Morgan Rhodes can write character growth. We no longer have this single minded girl, who was never able to think for herself. We now have this beautiful, empathic soul, who is constantly striving to be better. Cleo is so strong and would be completely capable of running her own kingdom.<br><br>In every one of these reviews I gush over <b>Magnus</b>, but the sentiment has held true over these four books; Magnus is everything I want in a male protagonist. Every book he gets stronger, and realizes his heart is capable and deserving of love. If pages 378 and 379 didn't make you feel <i>everything</i> that you've ever wanted in this series, then I don't really have words for you, because <i>that</i> was Christmas coming early for me. <br><br><i>“She was his princess. No. She was his goddess. With her golden skin and golden hair. She was his light. His life. His everything. He loved her more than anything else in this world.” </i><br><br><b>Lucia</b> is still fighting her many demons. She is now accompanied by the Fire Kindred, Kyan, who you very early on realize has his own agenda. She does find out much more about her birth family <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She has a sister named Laelia, who confides in her who their real father was: The old Paelsia ruler, Chieftain Basiliu. You know, the one her father screwed over, and then murdered, at the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1455382903" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. She also is carrying a very big secret with only herself, that will completely change this world and this story as we know it <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She's pregnant with Alexius' child. So the most powerful sorceress the world will ever know is now <i>also</i> carrying a Watchers' baby. How's that for new story arcs? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I also empathize a little more with Lucia during this book, but she's still <i>by far</i> my least favorite of the four.<br><br>Then we have <b>Jonas</b>, who just can't catch a break. The poor guy feels like everything he touches just fails <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and now he gets to deal with the mourning of Lysandra's death <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1455382903" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a>, Jonas was the character that held the most vengeance, and it made him blind to so many other things. I now feel like at this point in the story there has been a role reversal with him and the other three characters. Magnus has all the vengeance from trying to conquer not only his father, but also his kingdom. Cleo is constantly seeking vengeance for her family and friend's deaths. Lucia has more vengeance in her little body, than the whole freaking cast combined. Then we have poor Jonas, and it feels like he's just trying to get by and do the right thing, but it's always failing <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[at least now he has Felix back by his side <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Jonas also actually stands up for Cleo <i>and</i> Magnus when Nic tips off a new angst development that will surely happen in the following book <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Celo's first love, Theon, has a identical twin brother in Kraeshia. Nic tells him not only what happened to his brother, but that Magnus was the one to kill him <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>Amara, from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1471808405?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Gathering Darkness</a>, makes a huge appearance in <i>Frozen Tides</i>. She causes probably the biggest stir in this book, and it didn't have anything to do with her having obtained the Water Kindred in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1471808405?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Gathering Darkness</a> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She not only murdered her entire family back in Kraeshia, she also marries King Gaius! She does fall in love with Felix briefly before showing her true colors, but maybe he will be her undoing or her redemption <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Needless to say, she will make a huge impact in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1473732651?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">the fifth book</a>. I actually felt a lot of empathy towards Amara, and I think a lot of girls will probably feel the same. Even with her horrible actions you can always see <i>why</i> she doing the things that she does, because of everything she's been through. I don't really want to compare this series to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/976868255" rel="nofollow noopener">A Game of Thrones</a> anymore, because this whole world, and its characters, have grown <i>so</i> much and really became their own, but I have to say that Arama gives me the same feelings that Cersei gives me in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/976868255" rel="nofollow noopener">A Game of Thrones</a>. They are both villains who I have a great deal of feelings for, and I developed a huge love and hate relationship for both of them. <br><br>The Gaius prologue was something I didn't expect at all. Speaking of empathy, you will feel it for The King in this book, not as much as Amara, but you'll still feel some. You'll also discover a secret <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[that Gaius mother was not only a witch that started his infatuation with The Kindreds, but that she also took away the love of this life -- Cleo's mom <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, that will just make you believe that Cleo and Magnus are truly meant to be, and probably the best book couple I've ever read. <br><br>This book introduces us to a new witch named Olivia. She has been sent to the mortal realm by the last remaining Watcher in The Sanctuary, Timotheus, to watch over Jonas (mostly) and Nic. She not only does an amazing job <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[by saving Jonas' life <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, she plays a major role in the turn of events that happen as the end of this book <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[by telling Cleo and Magnus that The King was coming back with his new bride <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>I love these characters, and this whole world is very reminiscent of the way I felt while reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1454172046?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Harry Potter</a>. I'm not sure there is a bigger compliment that I could give to Morgan Rhodes, or this series, than that. I am completely infatuated, and cannot wait to see how this beautiful story will unfold. <br><br><a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://steamcommunity.com/id/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Steam</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany/profile" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5606511761162731689" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1871231750" />
    <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines"><img alt="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466111136p2/30004027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1871231750?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines">Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781101998984" href="/book/show/26856331-frozen-tides">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1871231750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17246658920936016583"><b>Dear Lord!</b><br/><u>This book just made it to my all-time favorites. Strong spoilers below</u><br/><br/>During the first three books, there were only two reasons why I kept reading this series, <b>the main and first one was Magnus</b>, and the second one was Magneo. They were the only chapters I was eager to read, the only ones that I couldn’t stop if I was in it <i>(and yes, even if it meant having to walk back to my place WHILE reading, hands freezing and bumping into strangers because I couldn’t pay attention to anything else</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17246658920936016583" style="display:none"><b>Dear Lord!</b><br><u>This book just made it to my all-time favorites. Strong spoilers below</u><br><br>During the first three books, there were only two reasons why I kept reading this series, <b>the main and first one was Magnus</b>, and the second one was Magneo. They were the only chapters I was eager to read, the only ones that I couldn’t stop if I was in it <i>(and yes, even if it meant having to walk back to my place WHILE reading, hands freezing and bumping into strangers because I couldn’t pay attention to anything else but those chapters)</i><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Because if you don't choose to fight against the wrong in the world, then you are the wrong in the world.”</i>
</blockquote><br>And then, <u>Frozen Tides</u> arrived, and it made my interest for the other characters grow. Yes, I’m not fooling myself, I know that I’m still here for the same <s>reasons</s> persons, but <b>the side stories were far more interesting. What I particularly like in this series is that the plot and characters don’t drastically change between one book and another. Each story is a fluid continuity to the previous one. New characters and plots are introduced smoothly.</b> Kraeshia, for instance, is gradually brought up. I loved that we finally got to see that new land as well as the way the Emperor decided to govern and rule his country. It also made me realize the problems I saw in the first books were nothing compared to the bigger scale. It helps to put things into perspective here. I especially liked that it took them two generations to fully organize their rebellion. It really shows the parallel to Jonas’ eagerness and that patience can be a strength. <br><br>The story starts where Gathering Darkness wrapped it off. <b>Cleo and Magnus fled in Limeros, as, after opposing King Gaius, they are guilty of treason</b>. Meanwhile, Jonas and Lucia are still in pursuit to find the dangerous Kindreds. In this book, Morgan Rhodes’ added two POV to the usual four: Felix and Amara. We met those two characters in the previous book, and they were both really mysterious, so I was happy to have their points of view here. I liked that Felix was both cocky and a badass assassin. He really grew on me and I started to fear for his life. <b>Amara is the ultimate villain, the female version of the King of Blood</b>. She is so driven by the power that she only sees through her selfish motives to be known and feared. She also seeks the Kindred, so that it would allow her to achieve her desire to dominate the world. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485171552ra/21789901.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485171552ra/21789902.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In Frozen Tides, everyone has something to fight for. <b>Lust for power is the main credo of this book</b>, characters want power for one reason or another: to seek revenge, to acquire freedom, to protect love, to find redemption, to belong. Most are willing to destroy everything and everyone in their wake to obtain it. Families were broken; new improbable alliances were made; loved ones were lost; all in this pursuit of power. And its unlimited power lies within the elemental crystals that are supposed to give infinite magic to the one that owns them. <br><br>I’m definitely in love with Magnus, <b>it pained me to witness his dark struggles, to feel his fear of being denied, his need to belong and be loved, his struggles with trust. The masks he is wearing are tiring him but it is his ultimate protection against rejection.</b> So he kept hiding his feelings especially to the principal interested (more or less successfully) and tried to conceal his good heart and soul while planning how to defeat his sadistic father and protect Cleo. I loved that we got to see his potential as a leader but I wanted more political situations where he could have taken strong and meaningful decisions. It could have been way easier on him if he was just like his father, and he tried to impose this thought on his mind but how it fails. Clearly, I could manage a book of only Magneo. <br><blockquote>
  <i>“Send me pain so I know I’m still alive. Help me continue to suffer. For if my father has already killed her, then I need to live so I can avenge her"</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485178895ra/21790738.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cleo has grown so much through the books. I like how <b>she became a master of manipulation.</b> She is brave and ingenious and keeps her chin up no matter the situation she is in. She never allowed Magnus or the King to minimize her, to lower her as a person. I loved how gradually she fell for Magnus and how she tried not to, especially with their mutual background. She slowly realized how caring and good he was, no matter what he pretended. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485171552ra/21789904.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Really, they could have made me die several times of heart attack with their sexual tension. <b>They are just so afraid of rejection that they NEED to push the other one away before being pushed away themselves</b>. Their cat and mouse game made me feel desperate and I just wanted to pull my hair off. But geez, it finally happened! This scene was just what I needed and beyond. My poor tortured soul, when he kneeled and made his declaration it was so raw, so powerful, my heart skipped a beat.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“I love you, Cleo," he said, the words finally coming to him, with no effort at all because of how true they were. "I love you so much it hurts."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457994538ra/18430069.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17246658920936016583" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_8069828'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8069828-the-crimson-crown"><img alt="The Crimson Crown (Seven Realms, #4)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1345041697l/8069828._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('b/rz9zbARDjV4x31mch18Qxjlmpd7HBloUWV3zngzcg0UE3clwDMnatGNsaVvc5bOj58xC+rpZY9404JDH8Hgw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('C5idnCsBo4/R4072fY8jWsNI7HjmYFVCSb093EfEtp9QMiO3isErKq9GZcVx+pjw9RUG1pQngLHVG+YKclt81A==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer2314874508893461964">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet vor</span>
  <span id="freeText2314874508893461964" style="display:none">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet voracious reader of all kinds of books. Under another pen name, she’s a national bestselling author of many paranormal novels. Falling Kingdoms is her first high fantasy. </span>
